RV agnimīḷe purohitaṃ yajñasya devam ṛtvijamRV hotāraṃ ratnadhātamamRV agniḥ pūrvebhirṛṣibhirīḍyo nūtanairutaRV sa devāneha vakṣatiRV agninā rayimaśnavat poṣameva divediveRV yaśasaṃ vīravattamamRV śatakratoRV dhanānāmindra sātayeRV yo rāyo vanirmahān supāraḥ sunvataḥ sakhāRV tasmā indrāya gāyataRV ā tvetā ni ṣīdatendramabhi pra gāyataRV sakhāya stomavāhasaḥRV purūtamaṃ purūṇāmīśānaṃ vāryāṇāmRV svarvatīrapaḥ saṃ gā asmabhyaṃ dhūnuhiRV āśrutkarṇa śrudhī havaṃ nū cid dadhiṣva me giraḥRV indra stomamimaṃ mama kṛṣvā yujaścidantaramRV vidmā hi tvā vṛṣantamaṃ vājeṣu havanaśrutamRV vṛṣantamasya hotaḥ pāvaka yakṣi caRV madhumantaṃ tanūnapād yajñaṃ deveṣu naḥ kaveRV adyā kṛṇuhi vītayeRV narāśaṃsamiha priyamasmin yajña upa hvayeRV madhujihvaṃhaviṣkṛtamRV agne sukhatame rathe devānīḷita ā vahaRV somapītayeRV devebhiryāhi yakṣi caRV ā tvā kaṇvā ahūṣata gṛṇanti vipra te dhiyaḥRV devebhiragna ā gahiRV indravāyū bṛhaspatiṃ mitrāgniṃ pūṣaṇaṃ bhagamRV ādityānmārutaṃ gaṇamRV pra vo bhriyanta indavo viśvebhiḥ somyaṃ madhvagna indreṇa vāyunāRV pibā mitrasya dhāmabhiḥRV tvaṃ hotā manurhito gne yajñeṣu sīdasiRV semaṃ no adhvaraṃ yajaRV yukṣvā hyaruṣī rathe harito deva rohitaḥRV tābhirdevānihā vahaRV ekamekaṃsuśastibhiḥRV adhārayanta vahnayo bhajanta sukṛtyayāRV bhāgaṃ deveṣu yajñiyamRV ihendrāgnī upa hvaye tayorit stomamuśmasiRV tā somaṃ somapātamāRV tā yajñeṣu pra śaṃsatendrāgnī śumbhatā naraḥRV mūrdhā nābhā soma vena ābhūṣantīḥ soma vedaḥRV agne vivasvaduṣasaścitraṃ rādho amartyaRV ā dāśuṣe jātavedo vahā tvamadyā devānuṣarbudhaḥRV juṣṭo hi dūto asi havyavāhano gne rathīradhvarāṇāmRV viśvadarṣataḥRV asi grāmeṣvavitā purohito si yajñeṣu mānuṣaḥRV ni tvā yajñasya sādhanamagne hotāram ṛtvijamRV manuṣvad deva dhīmahi pracetasaṃ jīraṃ dūtamamartyamRV yad devānāṃ mitramahaḥ purohito vā divas paryasme dhattaṃ puruspṛhamRV yan nāsatyā parāvati yad vā stho adhi turvaśeRV ato rathena suvṛtā na ā gataṃ sākaṃ sūryasya raśmibhiḥRV arvāñcā vāṃ saptayo dhvaraśriyo vahantu savanedupaRV navatiṃ dambhayo navaRV sa ghā rājā satpatiḥ śūśuvajjano rātahavyaḥ prati yaḥ śāsaminvatiRV ukthā vā yo abhigṛṇāti rādhasā dānurasmā uparā pinvate divaḥRV asamaṃ kṣatramasamā manīṣā pra somapā apasā santu nemeRV ye ta indra daduṣo vardhayanti mahi kṣatraṃ sthaviraṃ vṛṣṇyaṃ caRV tubhyedete bahulā adridugdhāścamūṣadaścamasā indrapānāḥRV vyaśnuhi tarpayā kāmameṣāmathā mano vasudeyāya kṛṣvaRV apāmatiṣṭhad dharuṇahvaraṃ tamo ntarvṛtrasya jaṭhareṣuparvataḥRV abhīmindro nadyo vavriṇā hitā viśvā anuṣṭhāḥ pravaṇeṣu jighnateRV sa śevṛdhamadhi dhā dyumnamasme mahi kṣatraṃ janāṣāḷindra tavyamRV rakṣā ca no maghonaḥ pāhi sūrīn rāye ca naḥ svapatyā iṣe dhāḥRV divaścidasya varimā vi papratha indraṃ na mahnā pṛthivīcana pratiRV bhīmastuviṣmāñcarṣaṇibhya ātapaḥ śiśīte vajraṃ tejase na vaṃsagaḥRV so arṇavo na nadyaḥ samudriyaḥ prati gṛbhṇāti viśritā varīmabhiḥRV indraḥ somasya pītaye vṛṣāyate sanāt sa yudhma ojasā panasyateRV tvaṃ tamindra parvataṃ na bhojase maho nṛmṇasya dharmaṇāmirajyasiRV pra vīryeṇa devatāti cekite viśvasmā ugraḥ karmaṇe purohitaḥRV sa id vane namasyubhirvacasyate cāru janeṣu prabruvāṇa indriyamRV vṛṣā chandurbhavati haryato vṛṣā kṣemeṇa dhenāmmaghavā yadinvatiRV sa in mahāni samithāni majmanā kṛṇoti yudhma ojasā janebhyaḥRV adhā cana śrad dadhati tviṣīmata indrāya vajraṃ nighanighnate vadhamRV sa hi śravasyuḥ sadanāni kṛtrimā kṣmayā vṛdhāna ojasāvināśayanRV jyotīṃṣi kṛṇvannavṛkāṇi yajyave va sukratuḥ sartavā apaḥ sṛjatRV dānāya manaḥ somapāvannastu te rvāñcā harī vandanaśrudā kṛdhiRV yamiṣṭhāsaḥ sārathayo ya indra te na tvā ketāā dabhnuvanti bhūrṇayaḥRV aprakṣitaṃ vasu bibharṣi hastayoraṣāḷhaṃ sahastanvi śruto dadheRV āvṛtāso vatāso na kartṛbhistanūṣu te kratavaindra bhūrayaḥRV eṣa pra pūrvīrava tasya camriṣo tyo na yoṣāmudayaṃsta bhurvaṇiḥRV dakṣaṃ mahe pāyayate hiraṇyayaṃ rathamāvṛtyā hariyogam ṛbhvasamRV taṃ gūrtayo nemanniṣaḥ parīṇasaḥ samudraṃ na saṃcaraṇe saniṣyavaḥRV patiṃ dakṣasya vidathasya nū saho giriṃ na venā adhi roha tejasāRV sa turvaṇirmahānareṇu pauṃsye girerbhṛṣṭirna bhrājate tujā śavaḥRV yena śuṣṇaṃ māyinamāyaso made dudhraābhūṣu rāmayan ni dāmaniRV devī yadi taviṣī tvāvṛdhotaya indraṃ siṣaktyuṣasaṃ na sūryaḥRV yo dhṛṣṇunā śavasā bādhate tama iyarti reṇuṃ bṛhadarhariṣvaṇiḥRV vi yat tiro dharuṇamacyutaṃ rajo tiṣṭhipo diva ātāsubarhaṇāRV svarmīḷhe yan mada indra harṣyāhan vṛtraṃ nirapāmaubjo arṇavamRV tvaṃ divo mahāmuruṃ vajreṇa vajrin parvaśaścakartithaRV avāsṛjo nivṛtāḥ sartavā apaḥ satrā viśvaṃ dadhiṣe kevalaṃ sahaḥRV nū cit sahojā amṛto ni tundate hotā yad dūto abhavad vivasvataḥRV vi sādhiṣṭhebhiḥ pathibhī rajo mama ā devatātāhaviṣā vivāsatiRV ā svamadma yuvamāno ajarastṛṣvaviṣyannataseṣu tiṣṭhatiRV atyo na pṛṣṭhaṃ pruṣitasya rocate divo na sānu stanayannacikradatRV krāṇā rudrebhirvasubhiḥ cadhenavaḥRV pṛṇantaṃ ca papuriṃ ca śravasyavo ghṛtasya dhārā upa yanti viśvataḥRV nākasya pṛṣṭhe adhi tiṣṭhati śrito yaḥ pṛṇāti sa ha deveṣu gachatiRV tasmā āpo ghṛtamarṣanti sindhavastasmā iyaṃ dakṣiṇā pinvate sadāRV dakṣiṇāvatāmidimāni citrā dakṣiṇāvatāṃ divi sūryāsaḥRV dakṣiṇāvanto amṛtaṃ bhajante dakṣiṇāvantaḥ pra tiranta āyuḥRV mā pṛṇanto duritamena āran mā jāriṣuḥ sūrayaḥ suvratāsaḥRV vibhrāṣṭimanu vaṣṭi śociṣājuhvānasya sarpiṣaḥRV yajiṣṭhaṃ tvā yajamānā huvema jyeṣṭhamaṅgirasāṃ vipramanmabhirviprebhiḥ śukra manmabhiḥ parijmānamiva dyāṃ hotāraṃ carṣaṇīnāmRV śociṣkeśaṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ dhanvāsahā nāyateRV dṛlḥā cidasmā anu duryathā vide tejiṣṭhābhiraraṇibhirdāṣṭyavase gnaye dāṣṭyavase pra yaḥ purūṇi gāhate takṣad vaneva śociṣāRV sthirā cidannā ni riṇātyojasā ni sthirāṇi cidojasāRV sukratuḥ purohito dame dame gniryajñasyādhvarasya cetati kratvā yajñasya cetati kratvā vedhā iṣūyate viśvā jātāni paspaśeRV yato ghṛtaśrīratithirajāyata vahnirvedhā ajāyataRV kratvā yadasya taviṣīṣu dadhurmanuṣyāsu vikṣu svarṇa citraṃ vapuṣe vibhāvamRV dadānamin na dadabhanta manmāgnirvarūthaṃ mama tasya cākanRV juṣanta viśvanyasya karmopastutiṃ bharamāṇasya kāroḥRV nitye cin nu yaṃ sadane śaryāmasanāmanu dyūnRV na yaṃ ripavo na riṣaṇyavo garbhe santaṃ reṣaṇā reṣayantiRV andhā apaśyā na dabhannabhikhyā nityāsa īṃ pretāro arakṣanRV mahaḥ sa rāya eṣate patirdannina inasya vasunaḥ pada āRV dadhire svābhuvaḥRV adha kratuṃ vidataṃ gatumarcata uta śrutaṃ vṛṣaṇā pastyāvataḥRV ā vāṃ bhūṣan kṣitayo janma rodasyoḥ pravācyaṃ vṛṣaṇā dakṣase maheRV yadīm ṛtāya bharatho yadarvate pra hotrayā śimya ahan vimimāno arkaṃ viṣurūpe payasi sasminnūdhanRV uta no hirbudhnyo mayas kaḥ śiśuṃ na pipyuṣīva veti sindhuḥRV yena napātamapāṃ junāma manojuvo vṛṣaṇo yaṃ vahantiRV uta na īṃ tvaṣṭā gantvachā smat uta na īṃ maruto vṛddhasenāḥ smad rodasī samanasaḥ sadantuRV pṛṣadaśvāso vanayaḥ na rathā riśādaso mitrayujo na devāḥRV pra nu yadeṣāṃ mahinā cikitre pra yuñjate prayujaste suvṛktiRV adha yadeṣāṃ sudine na śarurviśvameriṇaṃ pruṣāyanta senaḥRV pro aśvināvavase kṛṇudhvaṃ pra pūṣaṇaṃ svatavaso hi santiRV adveṣo viṣṇurvāta ṛbhukṣā achā sumnāya vavṛtīyadevānRV iyaṃ sā vo asme dīdhitiryajatrā apiprāṇī ca sadanī ca bhūyaḥRV ni yā deveṣu yatate vasūyurviRV pituṃ nu stoṣaṃ maho dharmāṇaṃ taviṣīmRV yasya trito vyojasā vṛtraṃ viparvamardayatRV svādo pito madho pito vayaṃ tvā vavṛmaheRV asmākamavitā bhavaRV upa naḥ pitavā cara śivaḥ śivābhirūtibhiḥRV mayobhuradviṣeṇyaḥ sakhā suśevo advayāḥRV tava tye pito rasa rajāṃsyanu viṣṭhitāḥRV divi vātā iva śritāḥRV tava tye pito dadatastava svādiṣṭha te pitoRV pra svādmāno rasānāṃ tuvigrīvā iverateRV tve pito mahānāṃ devānāṃ mano hitāmRV akāri cāru ketunā tavāhimavasāvadhītRV yadado pito ajagan vivasva parvatānāmRV atrā cin no madho pito vayaṃ pito vacobhirgāvo na havyā suṣūdimaRV devebhyastvā sadhamādamasmabhyaṃ tvā sadhamādamRV samiddho adya rājasi devo devaiḥ sahasrajitRV dūto havyā kavirvahaRV tanunapād ṛtaṃ yate madhvā yajñaḥ samajyateRV dadhat sahasriṇīriṣaḥRV ājuhvāno na īḍyo devānā vakṣi yajñiyānRV agne sahasrasā asiRV prācīnaṃ barhirojasā sahasravīramastṛṇanRV yatrādityā virājathaRV virāṭ samrāḍ vibhvīḥ duchunāyaiRV mādatvate daśate mādate no mā rīṣate sahasāvan parā dāḥRV vi gha tvāvān ṛtajāta yaṃsad gṛṇāno agne tanve varūthamRV viśvād ririkṣoruta vā ninitsorabhihrutāmasi hi deva viṣpaṭRV tvaṃ anarvāṇaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ mandrajihvaṃ bṛhaspatiṃ vardhayā navyamarkaiḥRV gāthānyaḥ suruco yasya devā āśṛṇvanti navamānasya martāḥRV tam ṛtviyā upa vācaḥ sacante sargo na yo devayatāmasarjiRV bṛhaspatiḥ sa hyañjo varāṃsi vibhvābhavat sam ṛte mātariśvāRV upastutiṃ namasa udyatiṃ ca ślokaṃ yaṃsat saviteva pra bāhūRV asya kratvāhanyo yo asti mṛgo na bhīmo arakṣasastuviṣmānRV asya śloko divīyate rodhacakrāḥRV sa vidvānubhayaṃ caṣṭe antarbṛhaspatistara āpaśca gṛdhraḥRV evā mahastuvijātastuviṣmān bṛhaspatirvṛṣabho dhāyi devaḥRV sa na stuto vīravad dhātu gomad viRV kaṅkato na kaṅkato tho sarve sākaṃ nyalipsataRV ni gāvo goṣṭhe asadan ni mṛgāso avikṣataRV ni ketavo janānāṃ nyadṛṣṭā alipsataRV eta u tye pratyadṛśran pradoṣaṃ taskarā ivaRV adṛṣṭā viśvadṛṣṭāḥ pratibuddhā abhūtanaRV
